The Great Battle on the Jinpu Line is About to Begin 80

Xuzhou correspondence: The date for the great battle on the Jinpu Line is approaching. It originated from the Jin army retreating to Nanyi and Dawenkou, and then gathering heavy troops at Taian. Recently, the Jin army on the Longhai Line was transferred to the Jinpu Line to reinforce it. According to reports, in addition to the original Chuan Zuoyi department, Sun Chu's department, which was transferred from Longhai, has built fortifications near Taian, relying on the mountains to occupy them, and deployed defenses at Nanyi and Dawenkou, as well as the Ningyang area. Therefore, now the Feng army is solely responsible for the defense of the Longhai Line. As for the Sun Dianying department in Bozhou, Luyi, and Zhecheng, the central army on the Longhai Line has been cleared and is also taking an offensive posture on the Jinpu Line. Various new forces have increased their strength to the front. Han's army on the Jiaoji Line and the various armies in western Shandong are taking considerable flanking attacks. Zhang Huichang, director of the Aviation Administration, also came to Xuzhou from Nanjing by plane Corbin yesterday morning (29th), and immediately went west from Xuzhou to meet with General Commander Chiang, and returned to Xuzhou that night. This morning (30th), he took a plane north to Yanzhou to command the air force's second team, Zhang Tingli's fourth team, Yang Guanyu's fifth team, Tian Xi's reconnaissance team, Mao Bangchu, and others, all of whom have sailed to Nanyi, Dawenkou, Taian, Ningyang, and other places to drop bombs. At the same time, He Yaozu was ordered by Zhuang to go west on the afternoon of the 29th with Chai Zuyin, Secretary of the General Headquarters, Chuan Ruizhe, Director of the Wounded Soldiers Inspection Office, and others, to report everything and handle military affairs on the way back. Today, military news from Jinpu is still silent, but the Central Army has taken an offensive posture, so the great battle will begin in the next few days. (30th)

The Province of Gansu Has Fallen into the Hands of the Gansu Army 81

_Wenhui Bao_, Gansu Correspondence, July 5th. The situation in Gansu has changed greatly in the past month. There have been two consecutive days of plentiful rain recently, the first rainfall of this scale in Gansu Province in three years. The people are exceedingly happy and hopeful for a good autumn harvest. Although the wheat harvest this year has not been good, it is expected that there will be no more famine after the autumn harvest. In the past, the province of Gansu suffered from banditry due to the weakness of the Feng army's defenses. Now the political situation has changed again. The Feng army has almost completely withdrawn from the province, and the counties have returned to the hands of the Gansu army. According to reports, this Gansu army is the old division of Zhang Zhaojia. After Feng Yuxiang's army was defeated at Nankou and retreated into Gansu, Zhang Zhaojia fled to Sichuan and traveled to Beiping via Hankou. His old troops also retreated into the mountains in the Northeast. The Feng army launched repeated attacks, but never succeeded. Until a month ago, when the Feng army went to Henan, the Gansu army reappeared, and they have been quite welcomed by the people wherever they have gone. It is said that their commander, De Gui (transliteration), is already near Lanzhou. Attention should be paid to this development, and it remains to be seen how it will be coordinated with other forces. Mr. Huang has also sent troops into Shaanxi to assist the Shaanxi army. It is said that Liu Yufen still has one division remaining in Shaanxi. The fierce fighting is now not far from Xi'an. Mr. Huang has declared his support for the National Government, and his soldiers treat foreigners very kindly, unlike the Feng army who were stationed in church schools and church properties.

○ Qingdao

Labor Unrest and Undercurrents in Party and Government 82

Qingdao Correspondence. Misunderstandings have arisen between the Party and the government in Qingdao City due to the rickshaw pullers' strike. The undercurrents have been quite strong in the past two days, and both sides have telegraphed the central government for instructions.

On the Party side, after more than one hundred rickshaw pullers went to the Party headquarters to petition on the 26th, and were arrested by the Public Security Bureau, the Party believes that the City Government is deliberately trying to undermine labor and disrupt Party affairs. Therefore, on the afternoon of the next day (the 27th) at 2:00 PM, an emergency meeting was convened. It was resolved to telegraph the central government to clearly order the punishment of Ge Jingen and to strictly order the City Government to release the arrested rickshaw pullers. At the same time, personnel were sent to comfort the arrested rickshaw pullers and to find ways to provide relief to the families of the arrested workers. The telegram to the central government is transcribed below: "The Qingdao Rickshaw Pullers' Guild colluded with the Social Affairs Bureau to forcibly increase rickshaw rentals by more than one-third. Rickshaw pullers were forced to strike. The City Government, disregarding the reputation of the government, sided solely with the capitalists, illegally disbanded the rickshaw pullers' union, and arrested rickshaw pullers everywhere, now totaling three or four hundred. Today, more than one hundred rickshaw puller representatives, formerly five hundred, were going to the City Government, which ordered more than five hundred armed police and plainclothes detectives to severely surround the Party headquarters as if facing a formidable enemy. Petition representatives were arrested as soon as they came out, forcing most representatives to take temporary shelter in the auditorium. At 3:00 PM, the armed police, under orders from their superiors, charged into the City Party headquarters with weapons and live ammunition. They arrested everyone indiscriminately, and those arrested were subjected to cruel beatings without exception. Committee members Li and Wu were imprisoned for a long time. Comrade Zhou Shenfu, secretary of the training department, was also detained. All offices and staff dormitories within the Party headquarters were thoroughly searched under the pretext of hiding reactionary elements, and countless important documents were lost. All internal and external communication of the Party headquarters was cut off, and the staff have lost their freedom of action. Such destruction of labor, creation of rear unrest, and disruption of Party affairs, recklessly risking reactionary wrongdoing, truly calls for tears over the future of the revolution. We implore you to immediately issue an urgent telegram to stop this and severely punish them to quell the public's anger. We are infinitely eager."

On the City Government side, the City Government's reasons are that it has received orders from the central government to suspend all labor movements during the military period. Now that the military situation at the front is tense, rear defense is especially important. The City Party headquarters is the highest Party organ in the city. The labor union cannot respect the orders of the central government and continues to engage in labor movement activities. The City Party headquarters should be stopped. How can the City Party headquarters, instead of stopping it, indulge in and protect the already resolved labor unrest by listening to the instigation of the labor union and convening a large number of workers at the City Party headquarters to hold secret meetings to incite the labor unrest? The City Party headquarters not only treats the orders of the central government as mere formalities, but also puts national affairs and the Party's position behind its mind. It has truly lost the qualifications of a Party member. In order to maintain local security, the City Government had no choice but to suppress it. Therefore, after arresting the petitioning rickshaw pullers, and because the _Republic Daily_ and the _Qingdao People's Daily_ were doing their best to publicize for the Party headquarters, reversing right and wrong and slandering the government, it was temporarily ordered to cease publication today, and the handling of the labor unrest was telegraphed to the central government. The telegram is as follows: (1) "At noon yesterday, the Industrial and Commercial Integrity Society coerced more than eighty rickshaw puller leaders to secretly deliberate in the Party headquarters auditorium to re-ignite the labor unrest and try to expand it. Many people were assigned to stop nearby police officers from reporting to the bureau. Bureau members were insulted and driven out. The situation was extremely serious. The Municipal Government had no choice but to request the Party headquarters to hand over the rickshaw pullers and send police to the auditorium where they were meeting to interrogate the rickshaw pullers separately. The most vicious elements who have been causing trouble in recent days are mostly inside, which further confirms that the labor unrest was indeed incited by those attending this meeting. Since disbanding the gathering, the city situation has gradually stabilized and the people's hearts have settled. If there are no complications, it should be able to end. However, the Party headquarters itself made the utensils in each room look messy and destroyed, and took videos, presumably to falsely accuse others. The police team, in handling this matter, did not enter any other place except for the entrance to the auditorium where the meeting was held. We are sincerely afraid of using falsehood to confuse the truth and fabricating reports to cause misunderstandings. In addition to ordering the bureau to carefully and cautiously release the people brought to the bureau for separate interrogation and to carefully prevent and maintain order, we respectfully report this by telegram." (2) "Li Yizhong, etc., appointed by the Qingdao Municipal Committee, secretly gathered rickshaw pullers to re-ignite the labor unrest, and even directed the staff to sabotage the Party headquarters and falsely accuse our department of doing so. Such rascality is truly unexpected. They are doing their best to publicize through the newspapers and news agencies they run, hoping to confuse the public. However, rumors of strikes and market closures in Qingdao City are rampant, causing alarm. Allowing them to reverse right and wrong and slander the government is feared to affect the people's hearts and concern the overall situation. We respectfully follow the Commander-in-Chief's instructions and temporarily order them to cease publication and prohibit the issuance of disruptive slogans and leaflets, etc., and await instructions from the central government. The rickshaw puller labor unrest in Qingdao City has now been completely quelled. Please release us from our worries and quickly grant us a thorough investigation to clarify the truth." A telegram was also sent to Committee Member Chen Guofu: "The rickshaw puller labor unrest has continued for seven or eight days. The police team has been on alert day and night, advising and exhausting themselves. We desperately hope for an early end. Yesterday, 80% to 90% had resumed work, but Li Yizhong, etc., re-induced more than eighty rickshaw puller leaders to secretly deliberate in the Party headquarters auditorium to re-ignite the labor unrest and try to expand it, and forbade the police and report bureau police teams to see what was already finished and would start again, which is especially worrying. We originally planned to wait for the rickshaw pullers to disperse to the Party headquarters entrance and separately summon them for interrogation, but Li realized this and did not allow them to go out. The bureau then reported to the Municipal Government and sent a letter to the Party committee to hand over the rickshaw pullers. Li then cursed and claimed that the rickshaw pullers were there to petition and that the police team was not allowed to do anything. The police team had no choice but to call the rickshaw pullers to the auditorium door and bring them to the bureau for interrogation. It was found that all the wanted thugs and instigators were inside, and according to their confessions, it was further confirmed that the labor unrest was indeed caused by the Party headquarters. At 2:00 PM, the first phase ended, and the city situation became more stable. Unexpectedly, Li then directed his staff to sabotage the utensils in each room and arranged them properly. He invited reporters and Comrade Zhang Daofan, etc., to view and pointed out that the police team had done it, causing Comrade Zhang, etc., to be almost deceived. In fact, the police team did not recklessly enter his room outside the auditorium. Moreover, since the rickshaw pullers had already been brought to the bureau, why would he sabotage it himself? A little calm observation would reveal the truth. We originally did not bother to argue about such rascal behavior, but we are afraid that rumors will be distorted and considered a weakness in the conflict between the Party and the government, causing comrades to feel pain and enemies and foreigners to laugh at us. Therefore, we especially enumerate this to hopefully inform the central government in detail." (28th)

Rioters in Xiamen Cause Disturbances 83

Xiamen Correspondence. Yesterday (the 25th), there were again rioters in Xiamen causing disturbances and looting the Salt Affairs Bureau's inspection station. Military police surrounded and attacked them, killing two. At the same time, prisoners in the Siming County Prison also took the opportunity to break out of prison, escaping twenty-eight people. Three have been recaptured. A part of Xiamen Port in Xiamen City is in turmoil, while the rest is very calm. The situation is recorded as follows:

Earlier, on the 24th, the military police authorities had received secret reports that rioters would cause disturbances the next day. That evening, Public Security Bureau Chief Zhang Xijie, under orders from the Command Headquarters, held an emergency meeting at the bureau. As a result, it was decided to divide the military police into different routes to lie in wait and strictly prevent disturbances in the Xiamen Port area. The deployment was divided into sections. The first section, the Penggong Temple area, was the responsibility of He Zhixing's unit of the Hutaizhou Battalion. The second section, the Dashengli area, was the responsibility of the Public Security Bureau's Security Team. The third section, the Chutoushan area, was the responsibility of Police Third Station Chief Wang Zongshi, who led the Browning pistol team. The fourth section, the Third Market area, was the responsibility of the Siming County Government's Detective Team and the Public Security Bureau's Detective Team. In addition, the First and Second Stations were responsible for maintaining security in Xiamen City. The deployment was completed at night. At about 7:00 AM on the 25th, three rioters suddenly came to the second floor of the Xiamen Salt Affairs Bureau's salt inspection station at the former Sijiangbieye Fish Market in Xiamen Port. Two of them went upstairs to the station chief's office. Station Chief Lin Buzhen and Accountant Lin Zuji were still in bed. The rioters first threw down the telephone receiver, leaving it hanging, so that there would be no ringing sound. Lin immediately woke up and threatened them with his hand, ordering them to hand over the money cabinet key and the uniform cabinet key. As a result, they only got the money cabinet key. At the time, the Salt Bureau employees were having breakfast in the downstairs living room. Two of them went upstairs, thinking they were visiting friends, and did not suspect anything. At the same time, there was a loud sound of firecrackers outside the bureau. The crowd went out to watch the excitement. One rioter outside the bureau raised a gun to stop them. The two rioters upstairs also went downstairs at this time and left together. The two Lins left the room and shouted that they had been robbed. The people downstairs were shocked, and the rioters used the firecrackers as a signal. The rioters outside the bureau scattered in all directions with propaganda leaflets. The Fish Market happened to be in the center of Xiamen Port. The military police who were lying in wait in various sections heard the sound of firecrackers and rushed to the scene in separate teams. At the same time, they sounded sirens. The rioters, about thirty in number, heard the sound and fled towards the back hill. The military police pursued them from behind. For a time, the sound of gunfire and firecrackers rang out. The Siming County Government's Guard Team at the foot of the hill behind the County Government saw the rioters escaping towards the County Government's back hill and also opened fire, and the rioters fired back, escaping up the hill. When the Fish Market incident occurred, the prisoners in the Siming Prison inside the County Government also rioted. The County Government's Guard Team was helping to attack the fleeing rioters and had no time to take care of the prisoners. More than 340 prisoners were able to escape. The prison guards were unable to control them. The prison doors were completely destroyed. They climbed over the walls and escaped to the back hill. Twenty-eight people escaped. Fortunately, the military police rushed to the scene, and the remaining prisoners dared not escape again. They repaired the prison doors while military police teams entered the mountains to search for the fleeing rioters. As a result, they captured a rioter in Western clothing on the Fish Market beach, carrying a hand grenade and propaganda leaflets, and shot him dead on the spot. Another worker-like person was captured by the military police while carrying a gun and distributing propaganda leaflets along the road. He was taken to the Fish Market beach and shot dead. The person in Western clothing was identified as Zhu Yuyi, a native of Pinghe. When the Fish Market riot occurred, he was frequently waving a gun in his right hand and a hat in his left hand, appearing to be directing the rioters, but his name has not been confirmed. Also, on the night of the 24th, the Maritime Public Security Bureau was ordered by the Command Headquarters to guard the sea. At about 4:00 AM the next morning, they used the First and Second steamships and several other hired merchant steamships to patrol the sea area near the Fish Market, Dashizi, the Electric Light Factory, and Xiamen University. Therefore, the rioters dared not escape to the sea after the incident, but escaped to the back hill. At about 8:00 AM, the Maritime Police saw a person in black shirt and pants, barefoot, running away on the Dashizi coast with a grenade wrapped in white cloth in his right hand. They captured him. He confessed that his name was Su Liancheng, a native of Huian. He was later taken away by the Command Headquarters. A total of twenty-eight prisoners escaped from the prison. Zhang Li and three others were recaptured. One person (named Zeng Yan, suspected of being a communist) was also shot dead in the back hill after he was captured. Eleven people were also captured near Xiamen Port, but their names have not yet been announced. (26th)

Contents of the New Sino-American Aviation Contract (Continued) 84

Section 4: Within seven days from the date on which this contract becomes effective in accordance with Section 2 of Article 9, both parties shall hold a meeting to formulate the articles of association, detailed rules and regulations, and establish a board of directors. All of the above shall be handled in accordance with this contract. Within fourteen days, the first board meeting shall be held, and the chairman and vice-chairman shall be elected in accordance with the above provisions. Section 5: The company shall have two supervisors, one appointed by Party A and one appointed by Party B. Article 4: Finances. Section 1: The company's share capital stipulated in Article 2 of this contract, as well as the company's revenue from air transport of mail, passengers, cargo, and other sources, shall be the company's assets and shall be deposited in a Chinese bank agreed upon by both parties. Section 2: After the company pays its operating expenses, the remaining funds shall be separately stored to prepare for the necessary expenses for increasing equipment and improvements, and dividends shall be paid to shareholders. However, dividends may be paid only after all of the company's operating expenses have been paid, debts and interest have been settled, and a sufficient public reserve fund has been set aside. Section 3: All expenditures of the company shall be paid by check. The check shall be signed by two persons appointed, one appointed by a director representing Party A and the other by a director representing Party B. Section 4: The company's bookkeeping and accounting shall use the latest type of system. The bookkeeping shall be in Chinese and recorded in Chinese as the basis, but it shall also be recorded in English when required by Party B. All books shall be audited monthly by a reliable registered accountant. Article 5: Air Routes. Section 1: The company shall operate the following air mail routes: Route 1: Shanghai-Nanjing-Jiujiang-Hankou-Yichang-Wanxian-Chongqing-Chengdu; Route 2: Nanjing-Xuzhou-Jinan-Tianjin-Beiping; Route 3: Shanghai-Ningbo-Wenzhou-Fuzhou-Xiamen-Shantou-Guangzhou. The company shall first open Route 1. After achieving success, it shall immediately open Route 2 and/or Route 3. If the company fails to open Route 2 and/or Route 3 within three years after this contract becomes effective, the company shall naturally lose the right to operate Route 2 and/or Route 3. However, this shall not apply if the company is unable to open these two routes within two years due to force majeure. Section 2: The company shall have the exclusive right to air transport all kinds of air mail on the above routes in accordance with the terms and conditions of the contract signed with the Chinese Postal Administration on the same day. Section 3: The postage for air mail and all regulations and rules for receiving and handling mail shall be handled in accordance with the contract signed by the company and the Postal Administration on the same day. Section 4: The company may also transport passengers and cargo on the above three routes, but it shall not hinder the safety and efficiency of air mail transport. Section 5: In the event of military necessity, the Ministry of Military Affairs may order the company's aircraft to deviate from fortresses and/or military important areas and fly on a safe route. Article 6: Operation. Section 1: After this contract is approved and effective, Party B shall immediately provide technical experience for Party A's use, be subject to its direction, and cooperate to promote the development of this business. Section 2: The company's fixed policy is to employ Chinese personnel as company employees, pilots, and mechanics. Party B shall provide Chinese people with ample opportunities to receive pilot training in China and the United States. At the same time, it shall provide Chinese people with ample opportunities to receive technical training as mechanics and radio operators, and to gain practical experience in all matters related to air transport. Section 3: Only aircraft and components of the best quality and latest type may be purchased, and goods manufactured in China shall be used as a priority. If goods manufactured in China are not available, products manufactured by the American Curtiss-Wright Airplane Company shall be used as a priority. However, all aviation goods worth more than 1,000 yuan in national currency shall be purchased by tender. Article 7: Airports and Landing Sites. Section 1: To the extent possible, Party A shall allow the company to use all airports and landing sites along the above routes, but the company shall pay reasonable rent. Section 2: If there are no airports and landing sites along the routes at necessary locations, the company shall be responsible for providing these facilities. Article 8: Radio. Section 1: In order to ensure flight safety, Party A agrees that the company has the right to install, maintain, and use appropriate radio telegraph and radio telephone transmitters and receivers, and agrees to provide the company with a considerable length of radio waves. This right regarding radio is exclusively for the company to transmit messages between stations and aircraft in order to maintain the efficiency of the company's business. However, all commercial communications and other communications that are not directly related to the company shall not be transmitted. Article 9: Contract. Section 1: Party A agrees to provide reasonable protection for all of the company's objects and other properties. Section 2: This company contract shall be signed by both parties and approved and filed by the National Government of the Republic of China, and shall become effective only after Party B has been formally notified in writing. Section 3: This contract shall be valid for a period of ten years from the date on which it becomes effective after approval. If neither party notifies the other party in writing of the termination of this contract one year before the expiration of the term, this contract shall continue to be valid for five years in addition to the ten-year valid period. Section 4: At the expiration of this contract, Party A shall have the right to fairly evaluate and purchase all of the company's properties. Section 5: If there is a dispute between the two parties regarding the contract, the dispute shall be submitted to arbitration. Each party shall appoint two arbitrators. The four arbitrators shall jointly appoint one impartial arbitrator. If the originally appointed four arbitrators cannot reach a majority agreement, the jointly appointed impartial arbitrator shall decide. Section 6: Party A, entrusted by the original China National Aviation Corporation, agrees with Party B that upon approval and effectiveness of this contract, the following contracts shall naturally be terminated and invalidated, and all rights stipulated or arising from those contracts shall be extinguished: (1) The air mail contract signed on April 17, 1929 between the original China National Aviation Corporation and the American Aviation Development Corporation (which contract was later transferred by the American Aviation Development Corporation to Party B); (2) The contract for the establishment and operation of aviation schools, factories, and air transport signed on April 17, 1929 between the original China National Aviation Corporation and the American Aviation Development Corporation (which contract was later entrusted by the American Aviation Development Corporation to Party B for cancellation in accordance with the law); (3) The airport gold coin loan contract signed on July 16, 1929 between the original China National Aviation Corporation and the American Aviation Development Corporation (which contract was later transferred by the American Aviation Development Corporation to the International Aviation Corporation and further entrusted by the International Aviation Corporation to Party B for cancellation in accordance with the law). The following promissory notes given by the original China National Aviation Corporation to Party B in accordance with the terms of the above-mentioned air mail contract shall be cancelled at the same time.

Installment Date Amount (calculated in gold coins) Installment No. 1 November 1, 1929 $13,670.57 Installment No. 2 December 1, 1929 $28,787.05 Installment No. 3 January 4, 1930 $17,059.61 Installment No. 4 February 1, 1930 $28,360.57 Installment No. 5 March 1, 1930 $32,871.29 Installment No. 6 April 1, 1930 $29,588.39 Installment No. 7 May 1, 1930 $32,069.56 Installment No. 8 June 1, 1930 $38,867.20 The original China National Aviation Corporation mentioned in this section was specially established by the National Government of the Republic of China on April 15, 1929 and is owned by the Chinese government. Section 7: This contract is written in both Chinese and English in four copies. Each party and the company shall hold one copy, and the remaining copy shall be submitted to the National Government of the Republic of China for filing. In the event of ambiguity in the interpretation of this contract, the Chinese contract shall be the standard for resolution. Section 8: This contract is binding on the legal successors of either party, but the successor must be a national of China or the United States. This contract is signed in Nanjing, Republic of China on July, 1930, which is July, 1930 in the Western calendar. Minister of Transportation of the National Government of the Republic of China Representative of American Air Transport Company (End)

○Zhejiang-Haiyan Ninghai Dike Failure Causes Disaster, Haining Correspondence. The Zongzihao stone dike near Xincang, Haiyan, experienced a dike failure on the 28th. Engineer Wang and engineers of the Haining Dike Works Bureau immediately supervised the workers to use mud bags and wooden stakes to block it as best as possible. However, the tide was so strong that it washed away again after twelve hours, and the seawater poured into the inner dike, becoming even more turbulent. On the evening of the 29th, the Junzihao Chenfenggang area, about eight li west of Zongzihao, was also washed away by the seawater, and the new dike (i.e., the Hangping Highway) was breached. Therefore, the Hangping Highway bus service has been suspended since the 30th. The breach is about two zhang four or five chi wide. The seawater flows into the inner river from the breach like a waterfall. The Yuanhua Dike River has already mixed with a large amount of seawater, which will have a significant impact on farmland. On the day of the dike failure, Mr. Dengke, an Austrian engineer from the Water Conservancy Bureau, and Engineer Wang of the Hanghai Dike Works Office both arrived at the construction site one after another to inspect and devise methods to repair the breach. The workers, including 200 hired from Hangzhou and 400 local workers, were busy carrying mud and driving piles. There were a total of twenty-seven cargo trucks from the Hangzhou Cargo Truck Company transporting sacks of mountain firewood day and night. They were working hard. As of the 31st, a total of 3,100 sacks and 40,000 bundles of mountain firewood had been used, which shows the scale of the project and the severity of the disaster. The dike opposite the Huaruemiao Temple, about twelve li west of Junzihao, also collapsed, and the seawater flowed in unabated. The seawater in the area near Junzihao is about eight chi above the mulberry fields, and all the crops there have been washed away. In total, the dangerous situation from Zongzihao to Panzihao is about twelve li, and it is about to become a major disaster. The Hanghai Dike Works Office has concentrated all its efforts on repairing the breach. They are working very hard. Unexpectedly, the stone dike from Xiaoputuo west of the near city to the seaside park was also eroded by the tide, with hundreds of holes and wounds, and the danger is alarming. The county Party headquarters, in view of the repeated collapses of the sea dikes and the imminent threat to the lives of the entire county, sent an urgent telegram to the province yesterday, requesting the Water Conservancy Bureau to expedite repairs to relieve the disaster.

Hangzhou Correspondence. The levees and dikes of the Hanghai Forts were severely damaged by the recent hurricane. More than ten zhang of the main dike was destroyed. Today (the 1st) at 8:00 AM, Secretary Jiang and Section Chief Zhu Chongguang of the Construction Department were dispatched to investigate. After arriving in Haining, Secretary Jiang and others met with Wang Shoubao, director of the Dike Works Office, to conduct an on-the-spot inspection of Jiubao and Shierbao. From the Haining bus station to Jiubao is about 20 li, and the mulberry fields along the way are lush. The breach there is in the inner dike, and the situation is relatively moderate. The damage is related to Shierbao, so the breach is only about two zhang, and it has already been repaired without any problems. From Jiubao to Shierbao is about 8 li, and the breach is in the outer sea dike, about twelve zhang. It was washed away by two angry tides. The first time, the stones of the main dike were washed away. The second time, the mud dike was washed away, and the tide poured into the inner dike. Now that the tide has receded, the water in the inner dike is pouring out towards the breach and retreating into the sea. Fortunately, the Dike Works Bureau had previously installed large strip stones under the main dike, otherwise the breach would have expanded. Now, after the Dike Works Bureau devised methods to repair it, the earthen dike was first reinforced with wooden piles and dike firewood, and mud was packed in sacks to fill the breach. After the water recedes completely, the stone dike will be repaired. There are hundreds of local people working there. If there are no major storms in the coming days, other problems should not arise. It is reported that the Construction Department believes that the losses from each angry tide washing away the dike are very large, and the cost of repairs every year is enormous. If the mountain in the middle of Biezimen were blasted away, the tide would be slowed down and would not cause such damage. The annual repair cost could also be saved. A fundamental solution is now being planned to achieve permanent stability.

Hangzhou Quick News 85

The price of grain in the Hangzhou market has been falling this past week. Rice sold by stores was reduced by four jiao per dan (unit of measure) from the day before yesterday. Now, due to the continuous wind and rain, the transport and sale of new grains from various places have been suspended, causing the price of rice in the market to suddenly rebound by about one yuan yesterday and today.

Yuyao is a special salt production zone, with more than 100,000 salt workers. Currently, the northwest districts of the county have reported banditry and smuggling. The Sixth Business Division has transferred salt police to suppress the situation. The Salt Yard Office has also consulted with the Weighing and Releasing Bureau staff to agree on joint defense measures. A report on the arrangements has been submitted to the province, stating that the local area is now calm.

Zhejiang Province has a total of four forest farms: the First Forest Farm in Xichao Township, Hangzhou, the Second Forest Farm in Jiande, the Third Forest Farm in Lishui, and the Fourth Forest Farm in Baiguan, Shaoxing. Now, in order to expand, the Construction Department plans to add branch farms in Dongtianmu, Cao'e, and other places. The expenses are planned to be allocated from the increased forestry fees in the 19th fiscal year. A proposal has been submitted to the provincial government for review and approval.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 86

Continuation of the Bandit Robbery Case in Hougang: It is reported that on the 30th evening, more than 30 bandits speaking local dialects suddenly arrived in Hougang Town, under the jurisdiction of the county. Carrying weapons, they raided Xu Yuxing's foreign goods store. The store owner, Xu Weiru, and two sons of a Mr. Wang (Wang Wangyun's sons) were kidnapped and taken away amidst shouts. It is said that the town had previously received a letter from the bandits demanding a ransom of 4,000 yuan to be delivered to a certain tavern next door to the Fourth Avenue in Shanghai, otherwise they would carry out kidnapping and robbery. At the time, everyone thought it was a threat, but it unexpectedly became a reality.

Tianmashan Sends Personnel to Re-seal: In the case of the Jiuxi Company's quarrying of stones in Tianmashan, the Agricultural Department ordered the county to seal it off for violating mining regulations. The county magistrate sent Inspector Zhang from the Public Security Bureau to implement the sealing. Unexpectedly, the mine operator refused to comply and continued quarrying. Recently, two stone crushing machines were newly transported from Shanghai and were about to be actively put into operation. The county government learned of this through investigation. Magistrate Jin believed that the merchant's defiance was improper, so he sent section member Qian Guangda together with Zhu Ying, the director of the Public Security Bureau, to the countryside one day to investigate. Since the responsible personnel of the company were all in Shanghai, they complied with the order and affixed county government seals to the front and back of the mountain. They also ordered the local land guard and the sub-station patrol leader to sign a guarantee, ordering them to stop the quarrying nearby. The two stone crushing machines were ordered to have the foreman instruct the Shanghai merchant to transport them back, otherwise they would be sealed off.

The General Clearing Bureau Officially Established: The local affairs of this county clearing out bandits has convened various meetings by the County Magistrate to prepare. Officially established at 9:00 a.m. one day, it is attached to the county government. Magistrate Jin concurrently serves as the director, Zhu concurrently serves as the deputy director, Li Zihua is the director of the first section, and Ni Guangrong is the director of the third section. The clerks and recorders of the bureau are Zhang Yinian and Ye Shaoyan, who originally held positions in the county government, to save on expenses.

Suzhou 87

Lake Bandits Appear Again at Taiping Bridge: In the area of Taiping Bridge, Shejiangkou, and Hongmiaotou in the county, there are more than 100 bandits appearing on boats, dispersing during the day and gathering at night, intending to rob Xiangcheng from the Yangcheng Lake entrance. Yesterday (the 1st), the district chief of the area submitted a request to the county government to send a team to suppress them.

Reassignment of Prison Warden: Yesterday, the Director of the Higher Court, Lin, received an order from the Ministry of Justice to dismiss Mei Guangfu, the warden of the Second Prison of Caohejing in Shanghai. The vacancy will be filled by Dong Changmin, the warden of the Fourth Prison of Nantong. The vacancy of the Fourth Prison will be filled by Sun Xiong, the current warden of the Changsha Local Court Detention Center.

Female Students of Jinan University Falsely Accused and Escorted to Zhenru, Shanghai: Fan Kangyuan, the secretary-general of Jinan University, reported to the local Public Security Branch on July 17th that female students Zhong Xiuying, Chen Jianru, Peng Miaoxian, etc., were secretly holding a meeting in Room 5 of the seventh dormitory, suspected of being reactionary. The branch immediately sent Patrol Leader Gu to lead the police to take the three female students Zhong Xiuying, Chen Jianru, and Peng Miaoxian to the bureau for a brief interrogation. The next day, the 18th, they were handed over to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for verification. As there were no suspicions after the interrogation, they were allowed to be released on bail. At that time, Peng Miaoxian was released on bail, but Zhong Xiuying and Chen Jianru were originally from Guangdong, and had no relatives in Shanghai, so they could not find a guarantor. On the 28th, the Public Security Bureau transferred them to the local court. After investigation, the prosecutor ordered them to be released on bail, but Zhong and Chen still could not find one. On the 1st, the police were dispatched to escort them to Suzhou and sent them to the Higher Court. Prosecutor Zhong Shangbin investigated and according to the statements, they were falsely accused because Fan Kangyuan, the secretary-general of Jinan University, was beaten by more than 100 students on July 14th, and then reported to the Public Security Branch on the 17th to have them taken away. After hearing the statements, Prosecutor Zhong ordered them to be sent to the Sijiang Street Detention Center to await interrogation as further investigation of evidence was required.

Wuxi 88

Four Children Drown While Practicing Swimming: Chen Huanwen, a resident near Chen Sifang in the tenth district of Xiyi (Beixiaxiang), is an elderly man who is deaf and works in farming. He has four sons and two daughters. The eldest son, Xianglin, is sixteen years old, the second son, Xiangfeng, is twelve years old, the third son, Xiangsheng, is seven years old, and the fourth son, Xiangzhen, is five years old. Except for the youngest son who has not yet entered school, the rest are all studying at a certain elementary school. Unexpectedly, yesterday afternoon, the four brothers Xianglin went to a nearby river to cool off and play. Before long, they saw village children swimming in the river in the distance. Xianglin, Xiangfeng, and Xiangsheng were eager to try, so they took off their shorts and went into the river to practice swimming. Unexpectedly, Xianglin and others did not know how to swim, and soon they drowned one after another. At that time, Xiangzhen, who was standing on the pier, saw this and was so anxious that he lost his footing and fell into the river and drowned instantly. Afterwards, Chen Huanwen and his wife learned that all four sons had died and were grief-stricken. Those who saw it were also saddened. They immediately bought four coffins and separately put them into coffins. It can be described as tragic.

The Case of Shooting Tan Qixuan Has Been Adjudicated: The case of Tan Qixuan, the former director of the Beishang Township Administrative Bureau of this county, being tragically shot and killed by bandits, has resulted in the county government successively arresting key criminals such as Lü Shiqiao, Bao Dayuan, Lü Genhu, Guo Asi, and Zhu Ada. After repeated summons and interrogations by Tang Yiqin, a member of the Committee for Clearing Accumulated Cases, the final debate was announced on the 25th of last month. Yesterday morning at 10 o'clock, the sentencing was held. Tang ascended to the criminal court and brought the five defendants, including Lü Shiqiao, to the court for sentencing. Lü Shiqiao was sentenced to death for the crime of inciting murder and deprived of all civil rights indefinitely. Bao Dayuan was sentenced to 20 years of imprisonment for the crime of jointly committing murder with premeditation and deprived of all civil rights indefinitely. Lü Genhu, Guo Asi, and Zhu Ada were each sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment for the crime of conspiracy to kill, and deprived of civil rights for seven years. At that time, Lü Shiqiao's face turned pale upon hearing the verdict and immediately declared that he would not accept it and filed an appeal, requesting that the judgment be delivered as soon as possible. Tang Jun approved it and immediately ordered them to be taken into custody for execution. Also, the defendant Sun Ruoxiu, after being transferred to Xiyi by the Higher Court, repeatedly requested a change of jurisdiction whenever the court was convened for interrogation, and claimed that he did not want to make any statements. Therefore, he was not sentenced yesterday. The case is now presented by Committee Member Tang to the Suzhou Higher Court for instructions and review.

The Municipal Public Property Management Committee Established: The Wuxi Municipal Public Property Management Committee stipulates that there will be seven committee members. County Magistrate Sun Zuji and Chen Liangdong, Director of the Finance Bureau, will be ex-officio members. The remaining five members were designated by people from various circles and are Qian Sunqing, Yang Hanxi, Li Diping, Chen Zhanru, and Cai Jiansan. After several preparatory meetings, Qian Sunqing was elected as the chairman. Yesterday (the 1st) at 8:00 a.m., Chairman Qian, accompanied by Committee Members Chen and Li, went to the former Municipal Preparatory Office to take over all documents related to municipal public property and held an establishment ceremony at the office, starting work on the same day.

Labor-Management Dispute in Silk Factory Resolved: The labor-management dispute in the silk factory in Xiyi has lasted for more than four months. The two sides have been at odds and have not been resolved. Recently, County Magistrate Sun convened meetings in stages to earnestly discuss and resolve the matter, obtaining opinions from all parties. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 p.m., a meeting was convened at the county government to continue mediation. Attendees included County Magistrate Sun Zuji, Zhang Hentian from the Party Consolidation Association, Liu Qidi from the Labor Consolidation Association, Cheng Jingtang from the County Chamber of Commerce, Gao Shufang representing the capital side, and Chen Peisan (represented by Hua Nianzu) and others representing the labor side, totaling more than 20 people. After five hours of discussion, an agreement was finally reached. Both sides made considerable concessions. As a result of the discussion, County Magistrate Sun summarized the opinions of all parties on the spot and made seven articles of agreement, and solicited the opinions of representatives of all parties, who signed them on the spot. The labor-management dispute in the silk factory was thus resolved.

Nantong 89

The County Government Advises the Business Community to Resume Business: Since the disturbances caused by thugs inside and outside Tongyi City, there have been many rumors, and major stores have not yet resumed business. On the 31st, the county government and the guard office agreed on measures to maintain public security and transferred police teams from the province and county to defend key areas. They also, together with the Tongchonghaitai General Chamber of Commerce, advised the business community to resume business as usual and issued a notice prohibiting rumors.

Flood Victims Along the River搶 to Build Breaches: The river dikes of Nantong Yaowang and various ports were breached in seven places by high tides. Baijiawei, Zhongsha, and dozens of miles around were flooded, with water depths of more than ten feet. By the 31st, the water had not yet receded, and strong winds and showers, followed by a raging tide, returned. The flood victims were extremely angry at the Construction Bureau's perfunctory attitude and delay. Each Wei took its own measures to rush to build breaches and took turns guarding them. The rice and other crops in the disaster area were submerged in the water for two days and nights, and there was no hope of survival. The autumn harvest was hopeless.

The Ministry of Military Affairs Stops Sending Wounded Soldiers to Tong: County Magistrate Zhang wired the Ministry of Military Affairs to request that the transport of wounded soldiers be stopped as the number of wounded soldiers transported has reached 1,600, and it is said that more are coming. A reply was received on the 31st approving the request.

Local Finances Difficult to Maintain: From the beginning of last year to the end of last month, the local finances of Nantong showed a deficit of 95,482 yuan in both revenue and expenditure. The above deficit was temporarily transferred from the property office. There is currently no way to make up for it.

All Circles Convene an Emergency Meeting: On the 31st, all local agencies and organizations in this county convened an emergency meeting at the county party headquarters to discuss the issue of public security in the city and countryside, and agreed with representatives of various tax offices to advance 20,000 yuan for the living expenses of the wounded soldiers. The amount of the advance payment was determined in proportion to the revenue of each tax collection agency.

Jiangyin 90

Conspiring to Kidnap Merchants, Bandits Released on Bail: Li Zonggang, Director of the Public Security Bureau, received a secret report from Xuan Jibao, a resident outside the east gate, that Li Yunbin, Xu Jinlong, and Xu Rongliang in Xicheng were gathering there, intending to go to Changshou Township to kidnap the son of the wealthy household Tan Nanshan. Director Li, upon receiving the report, led the police to arrest Li and others, and confiscated a pistol. They were taken to the bureau for interrogation for two hours. According to their confession, Inspector Li Hongze instigated the incident, and the pistol was borrowed by him. Director Li, considering the seriousness of the matter, did not want to investigate further, and released Xuan Jibao and the other four on bail, dismissing Li Hongze as a conclusion.

Xiagang Town Robbed by Bandits: Xiagang Town, eight miles from the city, which is the first police station of the fifth branch of the Public Security Bureau, was suddenly invaded by more than 30 bandits with guns at about 10 p.m. on the 31st. They rushed in and robbed more than a dozen guns from the police station. It happened to be raining heavily at the time, and they opened fire, wounding five patrolmen. The order on the streets was in chaos, and the losses were heavy. Because the telephone line was cut off, the news reached the city very late. The fifth district office sent a messenger to the city to report and dispatch a team to the countryside. The bandits were already gone.

Zhenjiang 91

Car Merchants Petition the Provincial Government Due to Price Cuts: The Zhenjiang rickshaw companies recently received instructions from the Construction Department to implement a price reduction for rickshaw rentals in the city and posted notices to inform the rickshaw pullers to implement it uniformly on August 1. The car merchants believe that since the provincial government moved to Zhenjiang, the prices of all goods have been high, and all industries are discussing price increases, but only rickshaw rentals are being reduced. In order to protect their capital, they find it difficult to accept this instruction. Therefore, yesterday, they hired lawyer Chen Liren to appeal to the provincial government. Moreover, there have been no recent disputes between labor and capital in this industry. Now, the sudden price reduction will inevitably lead to disputes.

New Prison Still Difficult to Construct: The Jiangsu Higher Court previously intended to build the Fifth Prison in Zhenjiang due to overcrowding in the prisons. It was estimated that it could accommodate a thousand people. The site has already been purchased with an advance payment, but the required funding is very large. An application for 300,000 yuan was previously made to the Department of Judicial Administration, and an instruction was received approving the transfer of 100,000 yuan from the Finance Department for temporary allocation. However, only 30,000 yuan has been received to date. After deducting the advance payment, there is not much left, which makes it impossible to start construction. Now, in addition to sending a letter to the Finance Department to expedite the allocation of the remaining funds, the Higher Court has also instructed the Zhenjiang county prison warden to build a bamboo fence around the perimeter of the purchased land.

Datada Taidong Salt Steamers Suspend Service: The Datada inland small steamer Taidong Salt route is currently suspended because all the servants on the steamers have gone on strike. It is also reported that the company's Da Xiang steamer encountered bandits at Caonianchang and the hull and machinery have been damaged and are being repaired.

New Rice Enters the Market, Prices Plunge: Recently, rice prices have gradually eased due to a good autumn harvest. Hundreds of stones of new rice were transported from Songjia Bridge, which borders Jiangnan, and entrusted to Yuandachang Rice Store for sale. The price of each stone of rice was set at 13 yuan. A large batch of new rice is continuing to be transported and is expected to fall sharply upon arrival.

Confiscation of Guns from the Xianzhen Merchant Corps: The 33rd Brigade stationed in Yangzhou sent a battalion commander to Xiannvzhen on the 28th to confiscate the guns of the town's merchant corps, together with the town's chamber of commerce and the district party headquarters, and arrested Tao Xuezhong, the captain of the corps, and brought him to Yangzhou. It is said that Tao Xuezhong was previously accused by someone, and the military and political organs arrested Tao and took him into custody. Guan Liting, a standing committee member of the town's chamber of commerce, invited Wang Jingting, the chairman of the county's chamber of commerce, to strongly intercede with the authorities and temporarily granted bail. The case is still intended to be investigated and verified. It is also heard that Standing Committee Member Guan rushed to Yangzhou on the evening of the 29th to visit County Magistrate Chen and Wang Jingting of the Chamber of Commerce to discuss the matter.

Wu's Collection of Books Allowed to Be Exempted from Retention: The Education Department reported that Wang Xiyou reported that Wu's collection of books on sea surveying was being sold and transported out, and requested that counties be ordered to retain them for preservation and national heritage. The county has ordered the Education Bureau to investigate and found that the collection of books is mostly ordinary household books from the imperial examination era, with no old Song and Yuan editions, and is not being sold abroad, etc. A special report was made to the Education Department, and instructions were received allowing the books to be exempted from retention. Yesterday (30th), the county presented a report to the Yangzhou Customs to separately instruct the customs checkpoints to verify and release them.

Jiaxing 93

County Government Secretary Accuses Business Firm, Case Dismissed: In Jiaxing, on June 10, 13, and 14, etc., the County Public Security Bureau ordered the police to forcibly conscript labor, and generally those with legitimate jobs were affected. At that time, County Magistrate Jiang was on leave due to business, and the county affairs were handled by Secretary Fang Zhuangyou. The representatives of the various legal groups repeatedly telegraphed the province requesting that County Secretary Fang Zhuangyou and Mo Runxun, Director of the County Public Security Bureau, be thoroughly investigated. Afterwards, Secretary Fang sued the business firms in court for falsely accusing him. The court prosecutor summoned both parties to court for interrogation on July 23. It is now learned that after the investigation, it was concluded that the elements of the crime did not have clear knowledge and intent, and it should be considered that there was insufficient suspicion of crime. In accordance with Article 244, Section 2 of the Criminal Procedure Law, the case was dismissed. The decision to dismiss was delivered to both parties for notification yesterday.

Hangzhou 96

Cloth Bureau Oversteps Authority and Detains Goods: The merchants in Zhejiang Province believed that the provincial Finance Department created the merchant-managed cloth donation tax to restrict the donation tax packages, and specially changed it to government-managed, setting up the Unified Cloth Donation Bureau, clearly defining the standards and ratios in order to verify and collect taxes. A General Bureau was established in the province, and a branch bureau was established in each region, appointing Hu Zutong as the director. Since the opening of the bureau, it has repeatedly mistakenly detained and levied excessive taxes on cargo transport outside of its scope. Merchants have requested the Finance Department to transfer orders for release based on reason. Recently, the Wenzhou branch bureau has again overstepped its authority and detained goods, and the local county party headquarters has reported the situation to the province, requesting the Finance Department to quickly stop it. The Finance Department believes that this is due to the bureau chief's improper employment and mismanagement. In addition to ordering the bureau not to engage in the aforementioned actions in the future, it is said that Bureau Chief Hu Zutong will be dismissed and replaced within days.

The Huge Fraudulent Gambling Case Is Handled: Xu Zhou, a native of Shaoxing residing in Dafuqing Lane in Hangzhou, has some assets. She was swindled out of 2,700 yuan by Xu Jifu, Lou Zhaorui, Zhu Jinshan, Zhong Santainiang, Zhang Guifang, and Zhang Yueting through fraudulent gambling. Xu Zhou realized this afterwards and reported it to the authorities. Lou Zhaorui, an important member of the fraudulent gambling gang, usually does all kinds of evil and has long been noticed by the authorities. After the report, he was caught by detectives from the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau in the Dongsheng Tea House, and Zhang Guifang and Zhang Yueting were also arrested at the same time and interrogated. Lou Zhaorui not only denied everything, but dared to falsely accuse detective Yuan Baichuan and others, saying that they had a personal grudge against him and framed him. Xu Zhou said that Lou had persuaded her on how to gamble and how to calculate, and then threatened her to pay the silver dollars, etc., all of which were done by Lou. Therefore, after interrogation, the detectives reported to Yan Youfu, director of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, that swindling a woman out of a huge amount of money was a heinous social phenomenon. Therefore, after a retrial, in addition to issuing a general order to his subordinates to arrest Xu Jifu and other criminals who were still at large, he yesterday transferred the criminals to the court. However, Lou Zhaorui has not been arrested, so his criminal behavior has not been confirmed, and he has been temporarily released on bail.

Building a Park at Liuhe Pagoda: Hangzhou Mayor Cai Zengji believes that Hangzhou is a place for tourists from China and abroad, and road administration should be given special attention. It has now been decided to build a direct asphalt road from the city station to the lakeside, and in addition to the six lakeside parks, there is no suitable place for rest and recreation. At present, it is planned to build a large park next to the Liuhe Pagoda in Jianggan, with tennis courts, basketball courts, etc. to promote sports, and to build a new-style swimming pool to stimulate interest in swimming.

Xiaoshan 97

Director of Finance Bureau Requests Suspension of Arrest, Not Approved: Shen Changyi, Director of the Xiaoshan Finance Bureau, was ordered by the Director of the Finance Department to be dismissed and handed over to the Hangzhou County Local Court for the crime of using public funds for private lending to Qianzhuang for interest. He was sentenced to one year in prison and fined 500 yuan in silver dollars and appealed. However, Shen requested to suspend his imprisonment because he had been in prison for a long time. The Criminal Court of the Higher Court ruled that the case concerned dereliction of duty by government officials and the suspension of arrest was not approved.

Director of Linpu Public Security Bureau Accused and Investigated: Since Li Yuan took office as Director of the Linpu Public Security Bureau in Xiaoshan, he has been out of touch with local public opinion. He was accused of gambling, smoking, and prostitution by citizens Tang Zhenqi and others. The provincial government ordered the Xiaoshan County Government to investigate and report back. County Magistrate Du previously ordered Yu Bin, the district chief of the Sixth District, to secretly investigate the case. Fearing that it was not true, the County Government has ordered Ge Shiyou, the District Chief of the Fourth District, to thoroughly investigate and report back for review.

Village Chief Illegally Collects Reporting Fees and Is Punished: Xu Naiguang, the village chief of Wujia Village in Xiaoshan, illegally collected land reporting fees of 2 jiao and 3 fen per mu, in violation of provincial orders. He was accused by villagers Sun Yuanshun, Ni Jinfu, and others to the provincial and county governments, requesting severe punishment. The County Government has transferred the case to the County Court for interrogation and investigation. However, Xu has filed a counterclaim, claiming that this was approved by the Chun County Government by a majority vote. The County Court ruled that the case involved violating provincial orders and privately collecting reporting fees, which the County Government would never have approved. It is evident that Xu's collection of illegal fees is corroborated by witnesses. He was sentenced to Article 360 of the Criminal Law, defining the crime of official corruption, and the sentence will be executed soon.

Two Children Die from Eating Fertilizer: On the 27th, four Sun children from Sunjia渡 in Southern Xiaoshan were working in the fields and came home hungry. They ate cold rice and saw a bag of fertilizer in the house. Thinking it was white sugar, they mixed it with cold rice and swallowed it. At night, two of the children fell ill, vomiting and having diarrhea non-stop. Two children died by dawn.

Education News 101

Important News

The deadline for filing private school applications is no later than the end of the summer vacation, i.e., the day before the start of the first semester of the 20th year.

An order from the Ministry of Education for the education authorities of all provinces and cities to comply with.

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued instructions to the education halls and bureaus of all provinces and cities to stipulate the deadline for filing applications for private schools at all levels in various places. Those who fail to file applications after the deadline will be ordered to stop enrollment or to close down. The original order is as follows: There are many private schools at all levels in various places. This ministry has repeatedly ordered them to file applications in accordance with the regulations. According to reports from various provincial and municipal education administrative agencies, some of these schools have submitted applications for filing, but many others are still waiting and watching. It is not appropriate to delay arbitrarily without complying with the regulations. Strict measures should be taken to clearly define the deadline for rectification. Except for private schools at all levels in the capital that have already been ordered by this ministry to file applications before the end of this summer vacation, i.e., before the first semester of the 19th year, the deadline for filing applications for private schools in all places should be promptly stipulated by the education administrative agencies of each province and city, taking into account the circumstances. However, the deadline for filing applications shall be no later than the end of the next summer vacation, i.e., the day before the start of the first semester of the 20th year. Those who fail to file applications after the deadline shall be ordered by the education administrative agencies of each province and city to stop enrollment or to close down, taking into account the circumstances. However, private schools in military and disaster areas, as well as remote areas, which are unable to comply with the regulations on time due to special obstacles, may have their extended deadlines drafted by the education administrative agencies of each province and city and submitted to the Ministry for verification and decision. In addition to distribution, this order is hereby issued to the Hall to immediately comply with and report the handling of the matter. Do not delay or play with it. This order.

Beijing City Private Schools Limited to File Before Summer Vacation 102

The Ministry of Education also instructed the Municipal Education Bureau to limit the period to before the summer vacation of this year for all schools to apply for filing. The original order states: It has been repeatedly ordered by the Ministry of Education to the education administrative agencies of all provinces and cities to urge the filing of applications for private schools at all levels in various places. According to the bureau's previous reports, many private schools at all levels in the capital have complied with the regulations and filed applications, but there are still some who are waiting and watching. It is not appropriate to arbitrarily delay without complying with the regulations. A deadline should be clearly defined for rectification. All private schools at all levels in the capital shall be required to comply with the regulations and file applications before the end of this summer vacation, i.e., before the start of the first semester of the next school year. Those who fail to apply for filing after the deadline shall be ordered by the bureau to stop enrollment or to prohibit the opening of new classes, or to be ordered to close down, taking into account the circumstances of each school, in order to emphasize the law and return to uniformity. This order is hereby issued to the bureau to comply with and to forward to all private schools at all levels under its jurisdiction that have not yet filed applications. The handling of the matter shall be reported at any time. This order.

Promotion of phonetic symbols in Mongolia and Tibet 103

The Ministry of Education previously announced measures for promoting phonetic symbols in various provinces and cities, but measures for promoting phonetic symbols in Mongolia and Tibet have not yet been formulated. The Mongolian and Tibetan Education Department of the Ministry of Education is currently drafting measures for promoting phonetic symbols in Mongolia and Tibet. In addition to annotating the national pronunciation to the right of Chinese characters, it is planned to annotate the meaning of Mongolian and Tibetan to the left of the characters, and to annotate the local sounds of Mongolian and Tibetan as much as possible. After these promotion measures are formulated and announced, a general order will be issued to various leagues and banners to set up phonetic symbol training institutes to expand training and facilitate promotion.

The Academia Sinica to Move Entirely to Nanjing Next Year 104

Due to the unresolved issue of the Qingliang Mountain site for the Academia Sinica, the Institute of Social Sciences and the Bureau of International Exchange of Publications, both located in Shanghai, have not yet been moved to Nanjing. Yesterday, a reporter interviewed Mr. Xu Weiman, the head of the Academia Sinica's affairs and director of the Bureau of International Exchange of Publications, at the Academia Sinica's general office. According to Mr. Xu, although the Qingliang Mountain site has been selected, the land price issue has not been satisfactorily resolved despite repeated meetings with the Land Bureau and landowners. Therefore, it is planned to construct a new building near the Astronomical Institute on the east side of Beijige to house the Institute of Social Sciences and the general office. Including the Astronomical Institute's library building, which is already under construction, the total construction cost is estimated to be around 100,000 yuan. The blueprints for the new building have been slightly modified, and the tender will be announced in about two weeks. Construction is expected to be completed in ten months, and it is anticipated that all institutes of the Academia Sinica will be moved to Nanjing by this time next year.

The Ministry of Education's Administrative Plan for the 19th Year, First Phase (2) 105

Regarding the beautification of education, improvement of customs, public entertainment, and public appreciation of objects:

1. Supervise provinces and cities in organizing opera, song, and drum-storytelling training classes to perform lyrics related to improving public morals and the national independence movement.

2. Supervise provinces and cities in implementing regulations for the censorship of dramas and films.

3. Supervise educational administrative organs in provinces and cities to issue public newspapers and weekly publications at low prices.

4. Issue a general order to national universities to appropriately add drama and music lectures or drama and music programs within the colleges of education or liberal arts, within the limits of available funding, to cultivate talents for improving drama and music.

Regarding public sports:

1. Continue to investigate the progress of public sports throughout the country and the various sports competitions and activities between social or group organizations.

2. Formulate public sports field regulations with reference to the existing sports facilities in provinces and cities.

3. Formulate a plan to promote sports nationwide and plan for the preparations for the Second National Games.

4. Convene sports experts to discuss issues related to sports field construction, the layout of jumping tracks and throwing areas, judging competition regulations, and various training and guidance methods.

Regarding special education and popular education:

1. Continue to investigate the relief efforts for the mentally and physically disabled nationwide and the reformatory education of prisoners.

2. Continue to review methods for implementing special education for the mentally and physically disabled, prisoners, etc., and consult with the Ministry of Judicial Administration.

3. Prepare for the internal work of the Central Education Museum, such as statistics, collection, and initial layout. Construction matters will commence immediately upon the Ministry of Finance's allocation of funds.

4. Collect popular reading materials and vernacular novels from the public, and request reports on practical family education and short educational film clips from both the United States and China.

5. Promote and reward provinces and cities for holding various lectures related to education, hygiene, or popular science during summer vacations.

Regarding general social education:

1. Organize the lyrics of the national anthem, hire veteran party and state officials to evaluate and select them, and submit them to the central government for approval.

2. Organize the social investigation forms sent by provinces and cities, classify and compile a national public education booklet.

3. Print and distribute the National Almanac for the 20th year.

4. Distribute the special publication of the First National Art Exhibition, "Art Exhibition," to promote art education.

Regarding Mongolian and Tibetan school education:

1. Supervise schools at all levels in provinces and cities to earnestly implement the regulations for the treatment of Mongolian and Tibetan students promulgated by the Ministry, and immediately enroll Mongolian and Tibetan students who apply for examinations.

2. Supervise the National Central University in preparing to establish Mongolian and Tibetan classes this year and revise the curriculum compilation table submitted by the university.

3. Issue a general order to the educational administrative organs of Mongolian and Tibetan banners and sects to investigate the number of public and private normal schools and the number of qualified teachers.

4. Issue a general order to the Mongolian and Tibetan banners and sects to select outstanding young people to study in inland normal schools, rural normal schools, or senior high school normal departments to cultivate appropriate teachers to serve in various regions of their banners and sects.

Regarding Mongolian and Tibetan public education:

1. Continue to order the Mongolian and Tibetan banners and sects to promote the literacy movement, extend adult literacy education, and report on progress within a specified period.

2. Issue a general order to the educational administrative organs of the Mongolian and Tibetan banners and sects to universally promote the National Phonetic Alphabet in the near future and establish National Phonetic Alphabet training institutes to assist in the movement to recognize Chinese characters.

3. Continue to investigate the popular songs, dramas, fables, myths, legends, etc., in the Mongolian and Tibetan regions, and compile and organize them. Design and improve textbooks for Mongolian and Tibetan schools and popular reading materials.

4. Continue to compile and print textbooks for schools at all levels in both Mongolian-Chinese or Tibetan-Chinese bilingual versions, or add Mongolian or Tibetan translations to existing textbooks (after being approved by the Ministry) and distribute them for application.

5. Create various simple educational propaganda materials with Mongolian or Tibetan translations attached and distribute them to schools in Mongolian and Tibetan regions to increase the knowledge of Mongolian and Tibetan youths and the public.

6. Select Mongolian and Tibetan women to translate party doctrine books and list them in Chinese.

Regarding compilation:

1. Continue to compile a vocabulary for public use.

2. Continue to translate scientific terms.

Regarding the review of textbooks:

1. Continue to review textbooks and teaching materials for all subjects in primary and secondary schools and public schools.

2. Continue to review children's reading materials.

3. Continue to review educational instruments and specimens.

4. Continue to review books on national humiliation history, diplomatic history, and books related to party doctrines.

Regarding educational statistics:

1. Complete the educational statistics for the 17th year.

2. Distribute the educational statistics survey form for the 18th year.

3. Compile statistics on university students nationwide.

4. Compile a list of secondary and higher schools nationwide. (End)

○ The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education Will Begin the Primary School Teacher Certification Exam: All procedures for the second session of the primary school teacher certification examination organized by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education were completed on July 30. Except for the exam dates, which are uniformly scheduled for August 7 to 9 in each district (the ninth district in Xuzhou will be temporarily postponed due to various reasons), the exam questions and papers for each district were dispatched yesterday by the staff of the Examination Committee and delivered to the chief examiners in each district for inspection. It is reported that the Provincial Department of Education has been extremely careful in reviewing qualifications and conducting the examinations. The exam questions are sealed with sealing wax and stamped with the name of the chairman. They cannot be opened until the exam begins. The examination schedule for each district has also been arranged and cannot be changed. On the morning of the 7th, there will be an exam on Party Doctrine and Mandarin; in the afternoon, there will be an exam on Natural Science Teaching Methods. On the morning of the 8th, there will be an exam on Educational Principles, School Administration, and Society; in the afternoon, there will be an oral exam. On the morning of the 9th, there will be an exam on Arithmetic; in the afternoon, there will be a physical examination. All examinees must arrive on time to take the exam. Latecomers will be included in the next session for re-examination. A total of 1,057 qualified examinees have passed the preliminary review in this session, covering 48 counties (no one from Bao Ying, Huai An, Tong Shan, Feng Xian, Pei Xian, Xiao Xian, Yang Shan, Pi Xian, Sui Ning, Dong Hai, Shu Yang, and Gan Yu; one person from Dongtai, whose qualifications still need to be verified, was not allowed to take the exam). In addition, 36 unqualified candidates and those who have not completed the procedures have been removed and must wait for the year-end holiday or the next session for supplementary examinations. The staff of the association have been working diligently during the summer, without rest even during holidays.

Hunan Province Urges the Implementation of Independent Educational Funding 106

Electing Members to the Promoting Committee

Changsha Correspondence: The issue of independent educational funding in Hunan Province has been advocated by educational personnel since the 13th year, but it has not yet been realized. Later, because the government vigorously maintained educational funding, in addition to allocating all the salt tax surcharge, it still found ways to raise the shortfall. Therefore, the heads of the schools did not rush to the government offices to request funding as before, but concentrated on the development of education, so that education in the 18th year had improved and was striving to expand. Now, because they feel that although the current government pays attention to educational funding, even a slight accident can fundamentally shake it, such as the influence of Gui's rebellion in Hunan, which has been affecting Xiangda for more than a month. Not only is there no funding for recurring expenses, but there is also not a single article for food expenses. Therefore, it is necessary to actively promote the independence of educational funding. Therefore, the principals, teachers, staff, and educational institutions personnel held a joint meeting at the Provincial Education Association on the 21st. More than 60 people, including Di Ang and Li Shiyuan, attended. Hu Yiru was elected as the chairman to report the reasons for the meeting, and then discussed each other for a long time and unanimously decided: (1) To organize the "Hunan Scholars to Promote Independent Education Funding Committee" and pass the organizational charter. (2) Elect Chen Runlin, Xiang Shaoxuan, Miao Yunan, Li Shiyuan, Hu Yiru, Li Yanjun, Lu Shengzhai, Di Ang, Luo Yi and other nine people as members. (3) The address of the Huang Association will be temporarily set up at the Provincial Education Association. (4) The expenses of this association will be shared by various schools. The meeting was adjourned and the adopted charter was recorded: Article 1: The purpose of this association is to promote independent education funding. Article 2: This association is jointly organized by all public and private schools and educational institutions in the province. Article 3: This association has nine members, who are elected by all public and private schools and educational institutions in the province. Article 4: This association has three standing members, who are elected by the members. Article 5: All members of this association are unpaid. Article 6: The staff of this association are concurrently held by the staff of the Provincial Education Association. Article 7: The expenses of this association are shared by all public and private schools and educational institutions in the province. Article 8: This association will convene an enlarged meeting of all public and private schools and educational institutions in the province when necessary. Article 9: The external documents of this association will borrow the seal of the Provincial Education Association. Article 10: This association will be dissolved when independent educational funding is implemented. Article 11: The charter of this association will be passed by a joint meeting of all public and private schools and educational institutions in the province and reported to the Department of Education for record and implementation.
